msg:In order to book a hotel with swimming pool, I chose Xiulan. When I checked the photos online, I felt that the bathroom was very shabby. In fact, the hotel room and bathroom facilities are very clean, comfortable, and not shabby. The photos are not as good as the actual effect. The room and bathroom are relatively large, and the bathtub should be about 1.7 meters long. The bed and pillow are very comfortable, and there are many choices of pillows such as 0 pressure pillow, buckwheat, lavender, etc. There are practical fruits, milk, yogurt, water, drinks, etc. for check-in, night bed, and check-out. The hotel front desk, room, and security services are all very warm and considerate. Parking downstairs is free and convenient. The Baoding Guild Hall on the first floor of the hotel is not rated high on Dianping, but our actual experience feels that it tastes good and the price is reasonable. Li Hongzhang's stewed vegetables, stir-fried water spinach, and stir-fried pot noodles are all delicious, and the taste is average. My family members all commented that this hotel is well booked. It is about 6 kilometers away from the Zhili Governor's Mansion by car, and it is quite convenient to go there by car.
